    /*-- Ajout de classes dans le body en fonction de la rֳ©solution --*/
 function initScreenResolutionClass() {
 var windowWidth = window.innerWidth;
 var body = $('body');
 var screenSm = 768;
 var screenMd = 992;
 var screenLg = 1367;
 body.removeClass('screenXs');
 body.removeClass('screenSm');
 body.removeClass('screenMd');
 body.removeClass('screenLg');
 if (windowWidth < screenSm) {
 body.addClass('screenXs');
 } else if (windowWidth >= screenSm && windowWidth < screenMd) {
 body.addClass('screenSm');
 } else if (windowWidth >= screenMd && windowWidth < screenLg) {
 body.addClass('screenMd');
 } else {
 body.addClass('screenLg');
 }
 }
 function getBreakPointSm(){
 return 768;
 }
 function getBreakPointMd(){
 return 992;
 }
 function getBreakPointLg(){
 return 1367;
 }
 /*-- APPEL DES FONCTIONS TESTS --*/
 function initTests() {
 initScreenResolutionClass();
 }
 $(document).ready(function () {
 initTests();
 });
 $(window).resize(function () {
 initTests();
 });
   </script>

           <script>
            $(document).ready(function(){
 window.redirectSearchPage = function(e) {
 window.location.href = computeUrl();
 return false;
 };
 window.initExpandSearchCalendar = function() {
 $("#daterangepicker").daterangepicker({
 "language" : "fr",
 "locale": {
 "format": "DD/MM/YYYY",
 "separator": " - ",
 "monthNames": moment.months(),
 "firstDay": 1
 },
 "showCustomRangeLabel": false,
 "alwaysShowCalendars": true,
 "autoUpdateInput": false,
 "opens": "embed"
 }, function(start, end, label) {
 computeInputTextCalendars(start, end, label);
 //redirectSearchPage();
 });
 };
 window.toggleHistoryOverlay = function() {
 if(getExpandSearchCookie().length === 0){
 return false;
 }
 };
 var computeInputTextCalendars = function(start, end, label) {
 var formatStart = 'Do MMM';
 if(start.isSame(end,'day')){
 $("#inputCalendars").val(start.format(formatStart));
 }else{
 var formatEnd = formatStart;
 if(!start.isSame(end, 'year') || !end.isSame(moment(),'year')){
 formatEnd = 'Do MMM YYYY';
 }
 $("#inputCalendars").val(start.format(formatStart) +'-'+ end.format(formatEnd));
 }
 };
 var computeInputTextThematics = function() {
 var inputThematicsValue = "";
 $('input[name="thematics"]:checked').each(function(index, input) {
 inputThematicsValue += $(input).data("classification-name") + " - ";
 });
 if ($('input[name="thematics"]:checked').length === 0) {
 $("#inputThematics").val("");
 } else {
 $("#inputThematics").val(inputThematicsValue.substring(0, inputThematicsValue.length - 3));
 }
 };
 window.clearThematics = function() {
 $('input[name="thematics"]:checked').each(function(index, input) {
 $(input).prop('checked', false);
 $(input).parent().removeClass('active');
 $("#inputThematics").val("");
 });
 //toggleClearThematicPicto();
 //removeOverlay();
 };
 window.clearSearchText = function() {
 $("#searchQuery").val("");
 if(!$("#clearSearchText").hasClass("hide")) {
 $("#clearSearchText").addClass("hide");
 }
 hideHistory();
 };
 window.clearDates = function() {
 $("#inputCalendars").val("");
 initExpandSearchCalendar();
 //toggleClearCalendarPicto();
 //removeOverlay();
 };
 var computeDateParameter = function() {
 var dateParameter = "";
 if($("#inputCalendars").val() !== "") {
 var dateUrlParameterName = "dates" + "=";
 $('.expand-search_date').find('input[name="daterangepicker_start"]').each(function(index, input) {
 dateParameter += dateUrlParameterName + $(input).val().replace(/\//g, '');
 });
 $('.expand-search_date').find('input[name="daterangepicker_end"]').each(function(index, input) {
 dateParameter += "&" + dateUrlParameterName + $(input).val().replace(/\//g, '');
 });
 }
 return dateParameter;
 };
 var computeUrl = function() {
 var searchUrl = window.location.protocol+'//'+window.location.hostname + "/place-spectacle/search-lt.htm";
 var parameters = computeParameters();
 return searchUrl + parameters;
 };
 var computeParameters = function() {
 var parameters = "";
 var classificationParameters = [];
 var searchParameters = $("#searchQuery").val();
 if (searchParameters !== undefined && searchParameters !== "") {
 setExpandSearchCookie($("#searchQuery").val());
 parameters += "q=" + encodeURIComponent(searchParameters);
 }
 var dateParameter = computeDateParameter();
 if(dateParameter !== ""){
 parameters += parameters !== "" ? "&" + dateParameter : dateParameter;
 }
 var classificationUrlParameterName = "type";
 $('input[name="thematics"]:checked').each(function(index, input) {
 if(parameters !== ""){
 parameters += "&";
 }
 parameters += classificationUrlParameterName + "=" + $(input).val();
 });
 if(parameters !== ""){
 parameters = "?" + parameters;
 }
 return parameters;
 };
 var searchSuggestionSelect = function(value) {
 $("#searchQuery").val(value);
 redirectSearchPage();
 };
 var computeHtmlHistory = function() {
 var histories = getExpandSearchCookie();
 $('#searchQueryHistory').html('');
 if (histories.length === 0) {
 var headingPanel = $('.expand-search-text').find('.panel-heading');
 if(!headingPanel.hasClass('hide')) {
 $('.expand-search-text').find('.panel-heading').addClass('hide');
 $('.expand-search-text').find('.panel-body').addClass('hide');
 }
 $('#searchQueryHistory').html('<li><span class="text">Vous n&#39;avez d&#39;historique de recherche.</span></li>');
 }else{
 for (i = 0; i < histories.length; i++) {
 var li = document.createElement("li");
 var a = document.createElement("a");
 a.onclick = function(){
 searchSuggestionSelect($(this).find(".text").text());
 };
 var text = document.createElement("span");
 text.className="text";
 text.innerText=histories[i];
 a.appendChild(text);
 li.appendChild(a);
 $('#searchQueryHistory').append(li);
 }
 }
 };
 window.deleteHistory = function() {
 createCookie('expandSearchSearchQueryHistory', '', -1);
 computeHtmlHistory();
 };
 window.hideHistory = function() {
 $('#searchQueryHistory').closest(".collapse").collapse('hide');
 };
 window.hideCalendar = function() {
 $('#daterangepicker').closest(".collapse").collapse('hide');
 };
 window.hideThematics = function() {
 $('.expand-search-genre').closest(".collapse").collapse('hide');
 };
 window.toggleHistory = function () {
 if($("#searchQuery").val().length > 0) {
 hideHistory();
 if($('#clearSearchText').hasClass("hide")) {
 $('#clearSearchText').removeClass("hide");
 }
 } else {
 $('#searchQueryHistory').closest(".collapse").collapse('show');
 }
 };
 var getExpandSearchCookie = function() {
 var history = [];
 if (readCookie("expandSearchSearchQueryHistory") !== "") {
 var cookies = JSON.parse(readCookie("expandSearchSearchQueryHistory"));
 for (var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
 history.push(decodeURIComponent(cookies[i]));
 }
 }
 return history;
 };
 var setExpandSearchCookie = function(searchQuery) {
 var previousCookie = [];
 var safeSearchQuery = encodeURIComponent(searchQuery);
 if (readCookie("expandSearchSearchQueryHistory") !== "") {
 previousCookie = JSON.parse(readCookie("expandSearchSearchQueryHistory"));
 }
 if(previousCookie.indexOf(safeSearchQuery) === -1) {
 var cookieToPlace = [];
 cookieToPlace.push(safeSearchQuery);
 for (i = 0; i < previousCookie.length && i <= 3; i++) {
 cookieToPlace.push(previousCookie[i]);
 }
 createCookie("expandSearchSearchQueryHistory", JSON.stringify(cookieToPlace), 30);
 }
 };
 function createCookie(name, value, days) {
 var expires = "";
 if (days) {
 var date = new Date();
 date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
 expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
 }
 document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
 };
 function readCookie(name) {
 var nameEQ = name + "=";
 var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
 for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
 var c = ca[i];
 while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
 if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
 }
 return "";
 };
 $(document).ready(function() {
 moment.locale("fr");
 initExpandSearchCalendar();
 });
 $("#formExpandSearch").ready(function() {
 $('input[name="thematics"]').click(function() {
 if($(this).is(':checked')){
 $(this).closest(".checkbox").addClass("active");
 }else{
 $(this).closest(".checkbox").removeClass("active");
 }
 computeInputTextThematics();
 });
 $("#formExpandSearch").submit(function(e) {
 e.preventDefault();
 });
 document.querySelector("#formExpandSearch").addEventListener('keypress', function (e) {
 e = e || window.event;
 if (e.keyCode === 13) {
 redirectSearchPage();
 }
 });
 computeHtmlHistory();
 });
 $('.expand-search-sup .expand-search-main').on('click', actionSlide);
 // $('#searchQuery').on('focus', function(){
 // $(this).removeAttr('placeholder');
 // });
 // $('#searchQuery').on('focus', function(){
 // $(this).data('placeholder',$(this).attr('placeholder'))
 // .attr('placeholder','');
 // }).on('blur', function(){
 // $(this).attr('placeholder',$(this).data('placeholder'));
 // });
 function actionSlide() {
 if ($(this).parent().find('ul').is(":visible")) {
 $(this).parent()
 .removeClass('current')
 .find('ul').slideUp();
 $('.expand-search-sup').removeClass('notCurrent');
 $('body').removeClass('open-widget-expand-search');
 } else {
 if ($('.expand-search-sup').hasClass('current')) {
 $('.expand-search-sup.current').removeClass('current').addClass('notCurrent').find('.expand-search-sub').slideUp();
 }
 $('body').addClass('open-widget-expand-search');
 $('.expand-search-sup').addClass('notCurrent');
 $(this).parent()
 .addClass('current')
 .removeClass('notCurrent');
 if($(this).parent().find('.expand-search-sub').children().length > 0) {
 if($(this).parent().hasClass('expand-search-recherche')) {
 if($("#searchQuery").val().length == 0) {
 $(this).parent()
 .find('ul').slideDown(800);
 }
 } else {
 $(this).parent()
 .find('ul').slideDown(800);
 }
 }
 }
 //return false;
 }
 $(document).click(function(e){
 var $this = $(e.target);
 if((!$this.closest('.expand-search-bloc').length) && (!$this.hasClass('glyphicon-chevron-left')) && (!$this.hasClass('glyphicon-chevron-right')) && ($('body').hasClass('open-widget-expand-search')) ) {
 $('.expand-search-sup').removeClass('notCurrent current').find('ul').slideUp();
 $(this).removeClass('open-widget-expand-search');
 }
 });
 });
           </script>

              $(document).ready(function() {

 }

 }
 });
 }, false);

              var hideTabsList = function(element){
 var dropdown = $(element).closest('.dropdown');
 dropdown.find('.dropdown-toggle>span.text').text($(element).text());
 dropdown.removeClass('open','active');
 $('.tabs div').removeClass('dropdown-backdrop');
 }

 var showLoader_6038491638514105674 = function () {
 $('#carousel-facet-6038491638514105674').addClass('overlay');
 $('#carousel-facet-6038491638514105674 > .widget-loader').show();
 };
 var hideLoader_6038491638514105674 = function () {

 $('#carousel-facet-6038491638514105674 > .widget-loader').hide();
 };
 var loadSlide_6038491638514105674 = function (swiper, widgetId, index, pageSizeToLoad,
 reloadAll) {
 if (reloadAll) {
 showLoader_6038491638514105674();
 }
 $.ajax({
 url: '/widget/carousel.do?widgetId=' + widgetId,
 type: "POST",
 dataType: "html",
 contentType: "application/json",
 data: JSON.stringify(
 {
 slideIndex: index,
 pageUrl: window.location.href,
 pageSize: pageSizeToLoad,
 languageId: '1',
 facets: facets6038491638514105674,
 filters: filters6038491638514105674,
 reloadAll: reloadAll,
 carouselFacetId: "6038491638514105674"
 }),
 }).done(function (responseText, textStatus, jqXHR) {
 if (jqXHR.status === 200) {
 updateSlider_6038491638514105674(swiper, responseText, reloadAll);
 } else if (jqXHR.status == 204) {
 updateSlider_6038491638514105674(swiper, responseText, reloadAll);
 $('#carousel-6038491638514105674').data('has-more', false);
 } else {
 $('#carousel-6038491638514105674').data('has-more', false);
 }
 });
 }
 ;
 var refreshFacets_6038491638514105674 = function () {
 for (var i = 0; i < filters6038491638514105674.length; i++) {
 var filterName = getTemplateName(filters6038491638514105674[i]);
 $('.selectedFacet6038491638514105674_'
 + filterName).text(filters6038491638514105674[i].libelle);
 }
 };
 var updateSlider_6038491638514105674 = function (swiper, responseText, reloadAll) {
 if (responseText && responseText.length > 0) {
 if (reloadAll) {
 var html = $.parseHTML(responseText);
 var htmlThumbnail = $(html).find('.swiper-wrapper');
 var htmlFacets = $(html).find('ul.widget6038491638514105674');
 if (htmlThumbnail.children().length > 0) {
 swiper.removeAllSlides();
 $.each(htmlThumbnail.children(), function (i, element) {
 element = $(element).find('.widget');
 if ($(element).hasClass('widget')) {
 var slide = $(
 "<div class='item carouselItem swiper-slide loaded '></div>").append(
 element);
 swiper.appendSlide(slide);
 }
 });
 $('ul.widget6038491638514105674').empty();
 $('ul.widget6038491638514105674').append(htmlFacets.children());
 refresh_6038491638514105674(swiper);
 refreshFacets_6038491638514105674();
 initCountdown();
 hideLoader_6038491638514105674();
 } else {
 swiper.removeAllSlides();
 initCountdown();
 hideLoader_6038491638514105674();
 }
 } else {
 var html = $.parseHTML(responseText);
 $.each(html, function (i, element) {
 if ($(element).hasClass('widget')) {
 var slide = $(
 "<div class='item carouselItem swiper-slide loaded '></div>").append(
 element);
 swiper.appendSlide(slide);
 }
 });
 initCountdown();
 refresh_6038491638514105674(swiper);
 }
 }
 };
 var refresh_6038491638514105674 = function (swiper) {
 var width = $(window).width();
 if (width <= 992) {
 $(swiper.nextButton).hide();
 $(swiper.prevButton).hide();
 } else {
 $(swiper.nextButton).show();
 $(swiper.prevButton).show();
 }
 };
 var lazyLoaderBeforeReachEnd_6038491638514105674 = function (swiper, reloadAll) {
 var widgetId = $('#carousel-6038491638514105674').data('widget-id');
 var actualIndex = geSlideDataIndex(swiper);
 if (reloadAll) {
 actualIndex = 0;
 }
 var maxSlideIndex = actualIndex + swiper.params.slidesPerView
 + (swiper.params.slidesPerGroup
 * 3);
 var realSwiperLength;
 if (swiper.params.loop) {
 realSwiperLength = swiper.slides.length - (swiper.loopedSlides * 2);
 } else {
 realSwiperLength = swiper.slides.length;
 }
 if (reloadAll) {
 realSwiperLength = 0;
 }
 var slideToLoad = (maxSlideIndex - realSwiperLength);
 var hasMore = $('#carousel-6038491638514105674').data('has-more');
 if (maxSlideIndex > realSwiperLength && hasMore) {
 if (slideToLoad < 1) {
 slideToLoad += 1;
 }
 loadSlide_6038491638514105674(swiper, widgetId, realSwiperLength,
 slideToLoad, reloadAll);
 }
 };
 function geSlideDataIndex(swipe) {
 var activeIndex = swipe.activeIndex;
 var slidesLen = swipe.slides.length;
 if (swipe.params.loop) {
 switch (swipe.activeIndex) {
 case 0:
 activeIndex = slidesLen - 3;
 break;
 case slidesLen - 1:
 activeIndex = 0;
 break;
 default:
 --activeIndex;
 }
 initCountdown();
 }
 return activeIndex;
 }
 var carouselSlider6038491638514105674 = new Swiper('#carousel-6038491638514105674', {
 initialSlide: 0,
 slidesPerView: 5.33,
 slidesPerGroup: 5,

 window.resetTermsFilter6038491638514105674 = function (type, name) {
 $('.selectedFacet6038491638514105674_' + type).text(name);
 }
 window.addTermsFilter6038491638514105674 = function (facetName, label, value, type) {
 $('.selectedFacet6038491638514105674_' + type).text(label);
 replaceExistingFilter6038491638514105674(type);
 var baseFilter = carouselTemplate6038491638514105674[facetName];

 window.addFilter6038491638514105674(
 Object.assign({}, {libelle: label, terme: value}, baseFilter));
 }
 };
 window.addFilter6038491638514105674 = function (filter) {
 filters6038491638514105674.push(filter);
 loadSlide_6038491638514105674(carouselSlider6038491638514105674,
 $('#carousel-6038491638514105674').data('widget-id'),
 0, computeMaxSlideIndex(), true);
 initCountdown();
 };
 var computeMaxSlideIndex = function () {
 return carouselSlider6038491638514105674.params.slidesPerView
 + (carouselSlider6038491638514105674.params.slidesPerGroup
 * 3);
 };
 window.replaceExistingFilter6038491638514105674 = function (type) {
 var indexType = -1;
 for (var i = 0; i < filters6038491638514105674.length; i++) {
 if (getTemplateName(filters6038491638514105674[i]) === type) {
 indexType = i;
 }
 }
 if (indexType >= 0) {
 filters6038491638514105674.splice(indexType, 1);
 }
 };

 for (var i = 0; i < filters6038491638514105674.length; i++) {

 }
 };
 window.removeFilter6038491638514105674 = function (index, type, name) {
 $('.selectedFacet6038491638514105674_' + type).text(name);
 filters6038491638514105674.splice(index, 1);
 loadSlide_6038491638514105674(carouselSlider6038491638514105674,
 $('#carousel-6038491638514105674').data('widget-id'),

 };
 var getTemplateName = function (filter) {
 for (var key in carouselTemplate6038491638514105674) {
 if (carouselTemplate6038491638514105674[key].id === filter.id) {
 return key;
 }
 }
 };
 })
 ;
 function initCountdown() {
 $('[data-countdown]').each(function () {
 if ($(this).children().length > 0) {
 return;
 }
 //Configuration
 var finalDate = $(this).data("countdown-date");
 var templateId = $(this).data("countdown-template") ? $(this).data("countdown-template")
 : "countdown-light-template";
 var startCallback = $(this).data("countdown-on-start") ? $(this).data("countdown-on-start")
 : "";
 var finishCallback = $(this).data("countdown-on-finish") ? $(this).data(
 "countdown-on-finish")
 : "";
 var translations = $(this).data("countdown-translations") ? $(this).data(
 "countdown-translations") : {
 totalDays: "days",
 hours: "hours",
 minutes: "minutes",
 seconds: "seconds"
 };
 var keys = ['totalDays', 'hours', 'minutes', 'seconds'];
 var template = _.template($('#' + templateId).html());
 var currDate = {totalDays: 0, hours: 0, minutes: 0, seconds: 0};
 var nextDate = {totalDays: 0, hours: 0, minutes: 0, seconds: 0};
 var countdown = $(this);
 var isCountdownInitialized = false;
 // Build the layout
 keys.forEach(function (key, i) {
 countdown.append(template({
 curr: currDate[key],
 next: currDate[key],
 key: key,
 label: translations[key]
 }));
 });
 // Return the time components that diffs
 function diff(obj1, obj2) {
 var diff = [];
 keys.forEach(function (key) {
 if (obj1[key] !== obj2[key]) {
 diff.push(key);
 }
 });
 return diff;
 }
 eval(startCallback);
 // Starts the countdown
 countdown.countdown(finalDate)
 .on('update.countdown', function (event) {
 var newDate = event.offset;
 var data;
 currDate = nextDate;
 nextDate = newDate;
 // Setup the data
 data = {
 'curr': currDate,
 'next': nextDate
 };
 // Apply the new values to each node that changed
 diff(data.curr, data.next).forEach(function (key) {
 var selector = '.%s'.replace(/%s/, key);
 var $node = countdown.find(selector);
 // Update the node
 $node.removeClass('flip');
 $node.find('.curr').text(data.next[key]);
 });
 if (!isCountdownInitialized) {
 keys.forEach(function (key) {
 var selector = '.%s'.replace(/%s/, key);
 var $node = countdown.find(selector);
 $node.find('.curr').text(data.next[key]);
 });
 isCountdownInitialized = true;
 }
 })
 .on('finish.countdown', function (event) {
 eval(finishCallback);
 });
 });
 }
                 </script>

 var lazyLoaderBeforeReachEnd_4457723602682265794 = function (swiper, reloadAll) {
 var widgetId = $('#carousel-4457723602682265794').data('widget-id');
 var actualIndex = geSlideDataIndex(swiper);
 if (reloadAll) {
 actualIndex = 0;
 }

 + (swiper.params.slidesPerGroup
 * 3);
 var realSwiperLength;
 if (swiper.params.loop) {
 realSwiperLength = swiper.slides.length - (swiper.loopedSlides * 2);
 } else {
 realSwiperLength = swiper.slides.length;
 }
 if (reloadAll) {
 realSwiperLength = 0;
 }
 var slideToLoad = (maxSlideIndex - realSwiperLength);
 var hasMore = $('#carousel-4457723602682265794').data('has-more');
 if (maxSlideIndex > realSwiperLength && hasMore) {
 if (slideToLoad < 1) {
 slideToLoad += 1;
 }
 loadSlide_4457723602682265794(swiper, widgetId, realSwiperLength,
 slideToLoad, reloadAll);

 function geSlideDataIndex(swipe) {
 var activeIndex = swipe.activeIndex;
 var slidesLen = swipe.slides.length;
 if (swipe.params.loop) {
 switch (swipe.activeIndex) {
 case 0:
 activeIndex = slidesLen - 3;
 break;
 case slidesLen - 1:
 activeIndex = 0;
 break;
 default:
 --activeIndex;
 }
 initCountdown();
 }
 return activeIndex;
 }

 var getTemplateName = function (filter) {

 ;
 function initCountdown() {
 $('[data-countdown]').each(function () {
 if ($(this).children().length > 0) {
 return;
 }
 //Configuration
 var finalDate = $(this).data("countdown-date");
 var templateId = $(this).data("countdown-template") ? $(this).data("countdown-template")
 : "countdown-light-template";
 var startCallback = $(this).data("countdown-on-start") ? $(this).data("countdown-on-start")
 : "";
 var finishCallback = $(this).data("countdown-on-finish") ? $(this).data(
 "countdown-on-finish")
 : "";
 var translations = $(this).data("countdown-translations") ? $(this).data(
 "countdown-translations") : {
 totalDays: "days",
 hours: "hours",
 minutes: "minutes",
 seconds: "seconds"
 };
 var keys = ['totalDays', 'hours', 'minutes', 'seconds'];
 var template = _.template($('#' + templateId).html());
 var currDate = {totalDays: 0, hours: 0, minutes: 0, seconds: 0};
 var nextDate = {totalDays: 0, hours: 0, minutes: 0, seconds: 0};
 var countdown = $(this);
 var isCountdownInitialized = false;
 // Build the layout
 keys.forEach(function (key, i) {
 countdown.append(template({
 curr: currDate[key],
 next: currDate[key],
 key: key,
 label: translations[key]
 }));
 });
 // Return the time components that diffs
 function diff(obj1, obj2) {
 var diff = [];
 keys.forEach(function (key) {
 if (obj1[key] !== obj2[key]) {
 diff.push(key);
 }
 });
 return diff;
 }
 eval(startCallback);
 // Starts the countdown
 countdown.countdown(finalDate)
 .on('update.countdown', function (event) {
 var newDate = event.offset;
 var data;
 currDate = nextDate;
 nextDate = newDate;
 // Setup the data
 data = {
 'curr': currDate,
 'next': nextDate
 };
 // Apply the new values to each node that changed
 diff(data.curr, data.next).forEach(function (key) {
 var selector = '.%s'.replace(/%s/, key);
 var $node = countdown.find(selector);
 // Update the node
 $node.removeClass('flip');
 $node.find('.curr').text(data.next[key]);
 });
 if (!isCountdownInitialized) {
 keys.forEach(function (key) {
 var selector = '.%s'.replace(/%s/, key);
 var $node = countdown.find(selector);
 $node.find('.curr').text(data.next[key]);
 });
 isCountdownInitialized = true;
 }
 })
 .on('finish.countdown', function (event) {
 eval(finishCallback);
 });
 });
 }
                 </script>

 var lazyLoaderBeforeReachEnd_8301511297984055118 = function (swiper, reloadAll) {
 var widgetId = $('#carousel-8301511297984055118').data('widget-id');
 var actualIndex = geSlideDataIndex(swiper);
 if (reloadAll) {
 actualIndex = 0;
 }
 var maxSlideIndex = actualIndex + swiper.params.slidesPerView
 + (swiper.params.slidesPerGroup
 * 3);
 var realSwiperLength;
 if (swiper.params.loop) {
 realSwiperLength = swiper.slides.length - (swiper.loopedSlides * 2);
 } else {
 realSwiperLength = swiper.slides.length;
 }
 if (reloadAll) {
 realSwiperLength = 0;
 }
 var slideToLoad = (maxSlideIndex - realSwiperLength);
 var hasMore = $('#carousel-8301511297984055118').data('has-more');
 if (maxSlideIndex > realSwiperLength && hasMore) {
 if (slideToLoad < 1) {
 slideToLoad += 1;
 }
 loadSlide_8301511297984055118(swiper, widgetId, realSwiperLength,
 slideToLoad, reloadAll);
 }
 };
 function geSlideDataIndex(swipe) {
 var activeIndex = swipe.activeIndex;
 var slidesLen = swipe.slides.length;
 if (swipe.params.loop) {
 switch (swipe.activeIndex) {
 case 0:
 activeIndex = slidesLen - 3;
 break;
 case slidesLen - 1:
 activeIndex = 0;
 break;
 default:
 --activeIndex;
 }
 initCountdown();
 }
 return activeIndex;
 }

 var getTemplateName = function (filter) {

 function initCountdown() {
 $('[data-countdown]').each(function () {
 if ($(this).children().length > 0) {
 return;
 }
 //Configuration
 var finalDate = $(this).data("countdown-date");
 var templateId = $(this).data("countdown-template") ? $(this).data("countdown-template")
 : "countdown-light-template";
 var startCallback = $(this).data("countdown-on-start") ? $(this).data("countdown-on-start")
 : "";
 var finishCallback = $(this).data("countdown-on-finish") ? $(this).data(
 "countdown-on-finish")
 : "";
 var translations = $(this).data("countdown-translations") ? $(this).data(
 "countdown-translations") : {
 totalDays: "days",
 hours: "hours",
 minutes: "minutes",
 seconds: "seconds"
 };
 var keys = ['totalDays', 'hours', 'minutes', 'seconds'];
 var template = _.template($('#' + templateId).html());
 var currDate = {totalDays: 0, hours: 0, minutes: 0, seconds: 0};
 var nextDate = {totalDays: 0, hours: 0, minutes: 0, seconds: 0};
 var countdown = $(this);
 var isCountdownInitialized = false;
 // Build the layout
 keys.forEach(function (key, i) {
 countdown.append(template({
 curr: currDate[key],
 next: currDate[key],
 key: key,
 label: translations[key]
 }));
 });
 // Return the time components that diffs
 function diff(obj1, obj2) {
 var diff = [];
 keys.forEach(function (key) {
 if (obj1[key] !== obj2[key]) {
 diff.push(key);
 }
 });
 return diff;
 }
 eval(startCallback);
 // Starts the countdown
 countdown.countdown(finalDate)
 .on('update.countdown', function (event) {
 var newDate = event.offset;
 var data;
 currDate = nextDate;
 nextDate = newDate;
 // Setup the data
 data = {
 'curr': currDate,
 'next': nextDate
 };
 // Apply the new values to each node that changed
 diff(data.curr, data.next).forEach(function (key) {
 var selector = '.%s'.replace(/%s/, key);
 var $node = countdown.find(selector);
 // Update the node
 $node.removeClass('flip');
 $node.find('.curr').text(data.next[key]);
 });
 if (!isCountdownInitialized) {
 keys.forEach(function (key) {
 var selector = '.%s'.replace(/%s/, key);
 var $node = countdown.find(selector);
 $node.find('.curr').text(data.next[key]);
 });
 isCountdownInitialized = true;
 }
 })
 .on('finish.countdown', function (event) {
 eval(finishCallback);
 });
 });
 }
             </script>

 'FAMILLE': {"@type": "TermeFiltre", "id": "MANIFESTATION_FAMILLE"},
 'SOUS_FAMILLE': {"@type": "TermeFiltre", "id": "MANIFESTATION_SOUS_FAMILLE"},
 'GENRE': {"@type": "TermeFiltre", "id": "MANIFESTATION_GENRE"},
 'PAYS': {"@type": "TermeFiltre", "id": "MANIFESTATION_PAYS"},
 'VILLE': {"@type": "TermeFiltre", "id": "MANIFESTATION_VILLE"},
 'DEPARTEMENT': {
 "@type": "TermeFiltre",
 "id": "MANIFESTATION_DEPARTEMENT_BILLETEL"
 },
 'REGION': {"@type": "TermeFiltre", "id": "MANIFESTATION_REGION_BILLETEL"}
 };
 var showLoader_1987865634661252422 = function () {
 $('#carousel-facet-1987865634661252422').addClass('overlay');
 $('#carousel-facet-1987865634661252422 > .widget-loader').show();
 };
 var hideLoader_1987865634661252422 = function () {
 $('#carousel-facet-1987865634661252422').removeClass('overlay');
 $('#carousel-facet-1987865634661252422 > .widget-loader').hide();
 };
 var loadSlide_1987865634661252422 = function (swiper, widgetId, index, pageSizeToLoad,
 reloadAll) {
 if (reloadAll) {
 showLoader_1987865634661252422();
 }
 $.ajax({
 url: '/widget/carousel.do?widgetId=' + widgetId,
 type: "POST",
 dataType: "html",
 contentType: "application/json",
 data: JSON.stringify(
 {
 slideIndex: index,
 pageUrl: window.location.href,
 pageSize: pageSizeToLoad,
 languageId: '1',
 facets: facets1987865634661252422,
 filters: filters1987865634661252422,
 reloadAll: reloadAll,
 carouselFacetId: "1987865634661252422"
 }),
 }).done(function (responseText, textStatus, jqXHR) {
 if (jqXHR.status === 200) {
 updateSlider_1987865634661252422(swiper, responseText, reloadAll);
 } else if (jqXHR.status == 204) {
 updateSlider_1987865634661252422(swiper, responseText, reloadAll);
 $('#carousel-1987865634661252422').data('has-more', false);
 } else {
 $('#carousel-1987865634661252422').data('has-more', false);
 }
 });
 }
 ;
 var refreshFacets_1987865634661252422 = function () {
 for (var i = 0; i < filters1987865634661252422.length; i++) {
 var filterName = getTemplateName(filters1987865634661252422[i]);
 $('.selectedFacet1987865634661252422_'
 + filterName).text(filters1987865634661252422[i].libelle);
 }
 };
 var updateSlider_1987865634661252422 = function (swiper, responseText, reloadAll) {
 if (responseText && responseText.length > 0) {
 if (reloadAll) {
 var html = $.parseHTML(responseText);
 var htmlThumbnail = $(html).find('.swiper-wrapper');
 var htmlFacets = $(html).find('ul.widget1987865634661252422');
 if (htmlThumbnail.children().length > 0) {
 swiper.removeAllSlides();
 $.each(htmlThumbnail.children(), function (i, element) {
 element = $(element).find('.widget');
 if ($(element).hasClass('widget')) {
 var slide = $(
 "<div class='item carouselItem swiper-slide loaded '></div>").append(
 element);
 swiper.appendSlide(slide);
 }
 });
 $('ul.widget1987865634661252422').empty();
 $('ul.widget1987865634661252422').append(htmlFacets.children());
 refresh_1987865634661252422(swiper);
 refreshFacets_1987865634661252422();
 initCountdown();
 hideLoader_1987865634661252422();
 } else {
 swiper.removeAllSlides();
 initCountdown();
 hideLoader_1987865634661252422();
 }
 } else {
 var html = $.parseHTML(responseText);
 $.each(html, function (i, element) {
 if ($(element).hasClass('widget')) {
 var slide = $(
 "<div class='item carouselItem swiper-slide loaded '></div>").append(
 element);
 swiper.appendSlide(slide);
 }
 });
 initCountdown();
 refresh_1987865634661252422(swiper);
 }
 }
 };
 var refresh_1987865634661252422 = function (swiper) {
 var width = $(window).width();
 if (width <= 992) {
 $(swiper.nextButton).hide();
 $(swiper.prevButton).hide();
 } else {
 $(swiper.nextButton).show();
 $(swiper.prevButton).show();
 }
 };
 var lazyLoaderBeforeReachEnd_1987865634661252422 = function (swiper, reloadAll) {
 var widgetId = $('#carousel-1987865634661252422').data('widget-id');
 var actualIndex = geSlideDataIndex(swiper);
 if (reloadAll) {
 actualIndex = 0;
 }
 var maxSlideIndex = actualIndex + swiper.params.slidesPerView
 + (swiper.params.slidesPerGroup
 * 3);
 var realSwiperLength;
 if (swiper.params.loop) {
 realSwiperLength = swiper.slides.length - (swiper.loopedSlides * 2);
 } else {
 realSwiperLength = swiper.slides.length;
 }
 if (reloadAll) {
 realSwiperLength = 0;
 }
 var slideToLoad = (maxSlideIndex - realSwiperLength);
 var hasMore = $('#carousel-1987865634661252422').data('has-more');
 if (maxSlideIndex > realSwiperLength && hasMore) {
 if (slideToLoad < 1) {
 slideToLoad += 1;
 }
 loadSlide_1987865634661252422(swiper, widgetId, realSwiperLength,
 slideToLoad, reloadAll);
 }
 };
 function geSlideDataIndex(swipe) {
 var activeIndex = swipe.activeIndex;
 var slidesLen = swipe.slides.length;
 if (swipe.params.loop) {
 switch (swipe.activeIndex) {
 case 0:
 activeIndex = slidesLen - 3;
 break;
 case slidesLen - 1:
 activeIndex = 0;
 break;
 default:
 --activeIndex;
 }
 initCountdown();
 }
 return activeIndex;
 }
 var carouselSlider1987865634661252422 = new Swiper('#carousel-1987865634661252422', {
 initialSlide: 0,
 slidesPerView: 4.0,
 slidesPerGroup: 4,
 nextButton: '.swiper-button-next',
 prevButton: '.swiper-button-prev',
 watchSlidesProgress: true,
 watchSlidesVisibility: true,
 breakpoints: {
 768
 :
 {
 slidesPerView: 2.33,
 slidesPerGroup: 2
 }
 ,
 992:
 {
 slidesPerView: 3.33,
 slidesPerGroup: 3,
 }
 ,
 1367:
 {
 slidesPerView: 4.0,
 slidesPerGroup: 4
 }
 },
 onAfterResize: function (swiper) {
 refresh_1987865634661252422(swiper);
 }
 ,
 onSlideChangeStart: function (swiper) {
 lazyLoaderBeforeReachEnd_1987865634661252422(swiper, false);
 }
 })
 ;
 lazyLoaderBeforeReachEnd_1987865634661252422(carouselSlider1987865634661252422,
 false);
 window.resetTermsFilter1987865634661252422 = function (type, name) {
 $('.selectedFacet1987865634661252422_' + type).text(name);
 }
 window.addTermsFilter1987865634661252422 = function (facetName, label, value, type) {
 $('.selectedFacet1987865634661252422_' + type).text(label);
 replaceExistingFilter1987865634661252422(type);
 var baseFilter = carouselTemplate1987865634661252422[facetName];
 if (baseFilter) {
 window.addFilter1987865634661252422(
 Object.assign({}, {libelle: label, terme: value}, baseFilter));
 }
 };
 window.addFilter1987865634661252422 = function (filter) {
 filters1987865634661252422.push(filter);
 loadSlide_1987865634661252422(carouselSlider1987865634661252422,
 $('#carousel-1987865634661252422').data('widget-id'),
 0, computeMaxSlideIndex(), true);
 initCountdown();
 };
 var computeMaxSlideIndex = function () {
 return carouselSlider1987865634661252422.params.slidesPerView
 + (carouselSlider1987865634661252422.params.slidesPerGroup
 * 3);
 };
 window.replaceExistingFilter1987865634661252422 = function (type) {
 var indexType = -1;
 for (var i = 0; i < filters1987865634661252422.length; i++) {
 if (getTemplateName(filters1987865634661252422[i]) === type) {
 indexType = i;
 }
 }
 if (indexType >= 0) {
 filters1987865634661252422.splice(indexType, 1);
 }
 };
 window.removeFilterFromType1987865634661252422 = function (type, name) {
 var indexType = -1;
 for (var i = 0; i < filters1987865634661252422.length; i++) {
 if (getTemplateName(filters1987865634661252422[i]) === type) {
 indexType = i;
 }
 }
 if (indexType >= 0) {
 removeFilter1987865634661252422(indexType, type, name);
 }
 };
 window.removeFilter1987865634661252422 = function (index, type, name) {
 $('.selectedFacet1987865634661252422_' + type).text(name);
 filters1987865634661252422.splice(index, 1);
 loadSlide_1987865634661252422(carouselSlider1987865634661252422,
 $('#carousel-1987865634661252422').data('widget-id'),
 0, computeMaxSlideIndex(), true
 );
 initCountdown();
 };
 var getTemplateName = function (filter) {
 for (var key in carouselTemplate1987865634661252422) {
 if (carouselTemplate1987865634661252422[key].id === filter.id) {
 return key;
 }
 }
 };
 })
 ;
 function initCountdown() {
 $('[data-countdown]').each(function () {
 if ($(this).children().length > 0) {
 return;
 }
 //Configuration
 var finalDate = $(this).data("countdown-date");
 var templateId = $(this).data("countdown-template") ? $(this).data("countdown-template")
 : "countdown-light-template";
 var startCallback = $(this).data("countdown-on-start") ? $(this).data("countdown-on-start")
 : "";
 var finishCallback = $(this).data("countdown-on-finish") ? $(this).data(
 "countdown-on-finish")
 : "";
 var translations = $(this).data("countdown-translations") ? $(this).data(
 "countdown-translations") : {
 totalDays: "days",
 hours: "hours",
 minutes: "minutes",
 seconds: "seconds"
 };
 var keys = ['totalDays', 'hours', 'minutes', 'seconds'];
 var template = _.template($('#' + templateId).html());
 var currDate = {totalDays: 0, hours: 0, minutes: 0, seconds: 0};
 var nextDate = {totalDays: 0, hours: 0, minutes: 0, seconds: 0};
 var countdown = $(this);
 var isCountdownInitialized = false;
 // Build the layout
 keys.forEach(function (key, i) {
 countdown.append(template({
 curr: currDate[key],
 next: currDate[key],
 key: key,
 label: translations[key]
 }));
 });
 // Return the time components that diffs
 function diff(obj1, obj2) {
 var diff = [];
 keys.forEach(function (key) {
 if (obj1[key] !== obj2[key]) {
 diff.push(key);
 }
 });
 return diff;
 }
 eval(startCallback);
 // Starts the countdown
 countdown.countdown(finalDate)
 .on('update.countdown', function (event) {
 var newDate = event.offset;
 var data;
 currDate = nextDate;
 nextDate = newDate;
 // Setup the data
 data = {
 'curr': currDate,
 'next': nextDate
 };
 // Apply the new values to each node that changed
 diff(data.curr, data.next).forEach(function (key) {
 var selector = '.%s'.replace(/%s/, key);
 var $node = countdown.find(selector);
 // Update the node
 $node.removeClass('flip');
 $node.find('.curr').text(data.next[key]);
 });
 if (!isCountdownInitialized) {
 keys.forEach(function (key) {
 var selector = '.%s'.replace(/%s/, key);
 var $node = countdown.find(selector);
 $node.find('.curr').text(data.next[key]);
 });
 isCountdownInitialized = true;
 }
 })
 .on('finish.countdown', function (event) {
 eval(finishCallback);
 });
 });
 }
             </script>

 var lazyLoaderBeforeReachEnd_3589901305821089364 = function (swiper, reloadAll) {
 var widgetId = $('#carousel-3589901305821089364').data('widget-id');
 var actualIndex = geSlideDataIndex(swiper);
 if (reloadAll) {
 actualIndex = 0;
 }
 var maxSlideIndex = actualIndex + swiper.params.slidesPerView
 + (swiper.params.slidesPerGroup
 * 3);
 var realSwiperLength;
 if (swiper.params.loop) {
 realSwiperLength = swiper.slides.length - (swiper.loopedSlides * 2);
 } else {
 realSwiperLength = swiper.slides.length;
 }
 if (reloadAll) {
 realSwiperLength = 0;
 }
 var slideToLoad = (maxSlideIndex - realSwiperLength);
 var hasMore = $('#carousel-3589901305821089364').data('has-more');
 if (maxSlideIndex > realSwiperLength && hasMore) {
 if (slideToLoad < 1) {
 slideToLoad += 1;
 }
 loadSlide_3589901305821089364(swiper, widgetId, realSwiperLength,
 slideToLoad, reloadAll);
 }
 };
 function geSlideDataIndex(swipe) {
 var activeIndex = swipe.activeIndex;
 var slidesLen = swipe.slides.length;
 if (swipe.params.loop) {
 switch (swipe.activeIndex) {
 case 0:
 activeIndex = slidesLen - 3;
 break;
 case slidesLen - 1:
 activeIndex = 0;
 break;
 default:
 --activeIndex;
 }
 initCountdown();
 }
 return activeIndex;
 }
 var carouselSlider3589901305821089364 = new Swiper('#carousel-3589901305821089364', {

 var getTemplateName = function (filter) {

 ;
 function initCountdown() {
 $('[data-countdown]').each(function () {
 if ($(this).children().length > 0) {
 return;
 }
 //Configuration
 var finalDate = $(this).data("countdown-date");
 var templateId = $(this).data("countdown-template") ? $(this).data("countdown-template")
 : "countdown-light-template";
 var startCallback = $(this).data("countdown-on-start") ? $(this).data("countdown-on-start")
 : "";
 var finishCallback = $(this).data("countdown-on-finish") ? $(this).data(
 "countdown-on-finish")
 : "";
 var translations = $(this).data("countdown-translations") ? $(this).data(
 "countdown-translations") : {
 totalDays: "days",
 hours: "hours",
 minutes: "minutes",
 seconds: "seconds"
 };
 var keys = ['totalDays', 'hours', 'minutes', 'seconds'];
 var template = _.template($('#' + templateId).html());
 var currDate = {totalDays: 0, hours: 0, minutes: 0, seconds: 0};
 var nextDate = {totalDays: 0, hours: 0, minutes: 0, seconds: 0};
 var countdown = $(this);
 var isCountdownInitialized = false;
 // Build the layout
 keys.forEach(function (key, i) {
 countdown.append(template({
 curr: currDate[key],
 next: currDate[key],
 key: key,
 label: translations[key]
 }));
 });
 // Return the time components that diffs
 function diff(obj1, obj2) {
 var diff = [];
 keys.forEach(function (key) {
 if (obj1[key] !== obj2[key]) {
 diff.push(key);
 }
 });
 return diff;
 }
 eval(startCallback);
 // Starts the countdown
 countdown.countdown(finalDate)
 .on('update.countdown', function (event) {
 var newDate = event.offset;
 var data;
 currDate = nextDate;
 nextDate = newDate;
 // Setup the data
 data = {
 'curr': currDate,
 'next': nextDate
 };
 // Apply the new values to each node that changed
 diff(data.curr, data.next).forEach(function (key) {
 var selector = '.%s'.replace(/%s/, key);
 var $node = countdown.find(selector);
 // Update the node
 $node.removeClass('flip');
 $node.find('.curr').text(data.next[key]);
 });
 if (!isCountdownInitialized) {
 keys.forEach(function (key) {
 var selector = '.%s'.replace(/%s/, key);
 var $node = countdown.find(selector);
 $node.find('.curr').text(data.next[key]);
 });
 isCountdownInitialized = true;
 }
 })
 .on('finish.countdown', function (event) {
 eval(finishCallback);
 });
 });
 }
             </script>

 // Prend en paramטtres l'URL cible et la fonction callback appelיe en cas de succטs
 function ajaxGet(url, callback) {
 var req = new XMLHttpRequest();
 req.open("GET", url, true);
 req.addEventListener("load", function () {
 if (req.status >= 200 && req.status < 400) {
 // Appelle la fonction callback en lui passant la rיponse de la requךte
 callback(req.responseText);
 } else {
 console.error(req.status + " " + req.statusText + " " + url);
 }
 });
 req.addEventListener("error", function () {
 console.error("Erreur rיseau avec l'URL " + url);
 });
 req.send(null);
 }
 //Interrogation pour perso nom et carte adherent
 function majMembre() {
 ajaxGet("/ws/WSMembre/getMembre", function (reponse) {
 var membreLog = JSON.parse(reponse);
 if(membreLog.prenom!=undefined){
 $(".header-tab-label.monCompte").text(membreLog.prenom);
 }
 if(membreLog.codeClientAdherent!=undefined){
 $(".header-tab-label.monCompte").before("<img class='cartePictoHeader' src='/static_lotus/uploads/nav/fnacspe/Images/Header/fnac-card.png' alt='Carte Adherent'/>");
 }
 });
 }
 function majPanier() {
 ajaxGet("/ws/WSPanier/getPanier", function (reponse) {
 var panierLog = JSON.parse(reponse);
 var maCroix;
 if(panierLog.nombreBillets>0){
 if(screen.width<750){
 $("#nombreDeBillet").css("display","inline");
 }
 $("#nombreDeBillet").text(panierLog.nombreBillets);
 var panierDecompte = new Date().getTime() + panierLog.dureeExpirationPanier;
 $("#timerPanier").countdown(panierDecompte).on('update.countdown', function(event) {
 var $this = $(this);
 $this.html(event.strftime('%M:%S'));
 var recupMinute = event.strftime('%M');
 var recupSecondeAvant = event.strftime('%S');
 $("#mesMinutesExpires").text(recupMinute);
 $("#mesSecondesExpires").text(recupSecondeAvant);
 var recupSeconde = recupSecondeAvant/60;
 var totalMinute = Number(recupMinute)+Number(recupSeconde);
 maCroix = 100-((totalMinute*100)/20);
 $('.ui-progressbar-value').css("height", maCroix + "%");
 if((maCroix>=75)&&(maCroix<=75.1)){
 $("#myModalPopInPanier, #overlayCustomMultiPanier").css("display", "block");
 }
 if((maCroix>=99)&&(maCroix<=99.1)){
 $("#myModalPopInPanier div, #myModalPopInPanier #FinaliserPanier, .blocDecomptePanier, #nombreDeBillet").css("display","none");
 $("#myModalPopInPanier p.expiration").text("Trop tard, votre panier a malheureusement dיjא expirי ! :(");
 $("#myModalPopInPanier, #overlayCustomMultiPanier, #myModalPopInPanier .fermetureDecompte").css("display", "block");
 $("#myModalPopInPanier .fermetureDecompte, .ico-panier").css("display", "inline");
 $(".monPanier").css("display", "inline-block");
 }
 });
 $(".blocDecomptePanier").css("display","inline-block");
 $(".blocDecomptePanier #barreFlag").css("display","block");
 }else{
 $(".monPanier, .ico-panier").css("display","inline");
 }
 });
 }
         </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     $(document).ready(function () {
 var EMAIL_PATTERN_MISSING_LEFT = new RegExp("[a-z0-9!#$%&'*+\/=?^_`{|}~-]+(?:\.[a-z0-9!#$%&'*+\/=?^_`{|}~-]+)*@");
 var EMAIL_PATTERN_MISSING_AT = new RegExp("@");
 var EMAIL_PATTERN_MISSING_RIGHT = new RegExp("@(?:[a-z0-9](?:[a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?)+");
 $('input#newsletterEmailInput').each(function(){
 var $this = $(this);
 $this.on('invalid', function(e){
 $this.addClass("newsletterInputError");
 if (!e.target.validity.valid) {
 e.target.setCustomValidity(computeErrorInputMessage(e.target.validity, e.target.value));
 }
 });
 $this.on('input', function(e) {
 $this.removeClass("newsletterInputError");
 e.target.setCustomValidity("");
 });
 });
 var computeErrorInputMessage = function (validityState, inputValue) {
 if(validityState.valueMissing) {
 return "Veuillez renseigner ce champ.";
 }
 else if(validityState.typeMismatch) {
 if(!EMAIL_PATTERN_MISSING_AT.test(inputValue)) {
 return "Veuillez saisir le caractטre '@'. L'adresse '%s' ne contient aucun '@'.".replace("%s", inputValue);
 } else if(!EMAIL_PATTERN_MISSING_LEFT.test(inputValue)) {
 return "Veuillez saisir la partie manquante avant le caractטre '@'. L'adresse '%s' est incomplטte.".replace("%s", inputValue);
 }
 else if(!EMAIL_PATTERN_MISSING_RIGHT.test(inputValue)) {
 return "Veuillez saisir la partie manquante aprטs le caractטre '@'. L'adresse '%s' est incomplטte.".replace("%s", inputValue);
 } else {
 return "Veuillez saisir une adresse email valide.";
 }
 } else {
 return "Veuillez saisir une adresse email valide.";
 }
 };
 $('.subscriptionNewsletter_subscribe').each(function(){
 var $this = $(this);
 $this.find("form").submit(function (event) {
 event.preventDefault ? event.preventDefault() : (event.returnValue = false);
 event.stopImmediatePropagation();
 $.ajax({
 url: '/ws/WSNewsletter/subscribe?email=' + $this.find('#newsletterEmailInput').val(),
 type: "POST",
 contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
 success: function(response){
 switch(response.returnCode){
 case 0:
 $this.find("form").fadeOut("fast", function() {
 $this.find('#newsletterSubscriptionInput_newsletterErrorMsg').remove();
 $this.find("form").after('<div class="row"><div class="newsletterResponseMsgContainer"><div class="newsletterResponseMsg col-md-16"><div class="newsletterResponseMsg" id="newsletterSubResponseMsg">' + response.msgResponse + '</div></div><div class="col-md-8 newsletterResponsePicto"><span class="icon"><i class="fonticon fonticon-check fonticon48"></i></span></div></div></div>');
 $this.find('.newsletterResponseMsgContainer').fadeTo("slow",1);
 });
 break;
 case 80:
 $this.find('#newsletterEmailInput').addClass("newsletterInputError");
 $this.find('#newsletterSubscriptionInput_newsletterErrorMsg').remove();
 $this.find("form").after('<div class="row" id="newsletterSubscriptionInput_newsletterErrorMsg"><div class="newsletterSubscriptionInput"><span class="newsletterErrorMsg" id="msgErrorSubscribe"></span></div></div>');
 $this.find('#msgErrorSubscribe').empty();
 $this.find('#msgErrorSubscribe').append(response.msgResponse);
 break;
 case 100:
 $this.find('#newsletterEmailInput').addClass("newsletterInputError");
 $this.find('#newsletterSubscriptionInput_newsletterErrorMsg').remove();
 $this.find("form").after('<div class="row" id="newsletterSubscriptionInput_newsletterErrorMsg"><div class="newsletterSubscriptionInput"><span class="newsletterErrorMsg" id="msgErrorSubscribe"></span></div></div>');
 $this.find('#msgErrorSubscribe').append(response.msgResponse);
 break;
 }
 }
 });
 return false;
 });
 });
 $('.subscriptionNewsletter_unsubscribe').each(function(form){
 var $this = $(this);
 $this.find("form").submit(function (event) {
 event.preventDefault ? event.preventDefault() : (event.returnValue = false);
 event.stopImmediatePropagation();
 $.ajax({
 url: '/ws/WSNewsletter/unsubscribe?email=' + $this.find('#newsletterEmailInput').val(),
 type: "POST",
 contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
 success: function(response){
 switch(response.returnCode){
 case 0:
 $this.find("form").fadeOut("fast", function() {
 $this.find('#newsletterSubscriptionInput_msgErrorUnsubscribe').remove();
 $this.find("form").after('<div class="row"><div class="newsletterResponseMsgContainer"><div class="newsletterResponseMsg col-md-16"><div class="newsletterResponseMsg" id="newsletterUnsubResponseMsg">' + response.msgResponse + '</div></div><div class="col-md-8 newsletterResponsePicto"><span class="icon"><i class="fonticon fonticon-check fonticon48"></i></span></div></div></div>');
 $this.find('.newsletterResponseMsgContainer').fadeTo("slow",1);
 });
 break;
 case 99:
 $this.find('#newsletterEmailInput').addClass("newsletterInputError");
 $this.find('#newsletterSubscriptionInput_msgErrorUnsubscribe').remove();
 $this.find("form").after('<div class="row" id="newsletterSubscriptionInput_msgErrorUnsubscribe"><div class="newsletterSubscriptionInput"><span class="newsletterErrorMsg" id="msgErrorUnsubscribe"></span></div></div>');
 $this.find('#msgErrorUnsubscribe').append(response.msgResponse);
 break;
 case 100:
 $this.find('#newsletterEmailInput').addClass("newsletterInputError");
 $this.find('#newsletterSubscriptionInput_msgErrorUnsubscribe').remove();
 $this.find("form").after('<div class="row" id="newsletterSubscriptionInput_msgErrorUnsubscribe"><div class="newsletterSubscriptionInput"><span class="newsletterErrorMsg" id="msgErrorUnsubscribe"></span></div></div>');
 $this.find('#msgErrorUnsubscribe').append(response.msgResponse);
 break;
 }
 }
 });
 return false;
 });
 });
